[REVIEW_RETELLING] Laura Sugamele, Università degli Studi "La Sapienza" di Roma ( https://uniroma1.academia.edu/LauraSugamele ) — http://dialetticaefilosofia.it/public/pdf/74recensione.pdf

[REVIEW_RETELLING] Rodrigo Farias de Sousa, Doutor em História. Professor de História IUPERJ/UCAM — https://periodicos.unifap.br/index.php/fronteiras/article/download/3188/rodrigov2n2.pdf — «O foco do autor são os Estados Unidos e a Europa, particularmente a do Leste, e mal sefala dos chamados regimes populistas latino-americanos:Perón só é citado uma vez, e Vargase Cárdenas, nem isso.»

Merényi Miklós, Corvinus University of Budapest ( https://uni-corvinus.academia.edu/mrnymkls ) — https://www.ceeol.com/search/viewpdf?id=609633 — «Azonban Müller könyve – talán a terjedelmi okok és a fentiekből fakadó diplo matikusság miatt – kevés fogódzóval szolgál annak elkerülésére, hogy egy másik szinten visszahulljunk a semleges szakértő objektiváló szerepébe. A szerző ugyanis a mű feszes mondanivalója mellett csak homályos utalásokat tesz arra, hogyan foglal állást abban a gyakorlatias kompromisszumban, amelyet a demokratikus rendszert veszélyeztető képviseleti igények megfékezése és ezen igények, mint a „népakarat” szükségszerű kifejeződései között kell elgondolnunk. Müller könyve ezzel együtt érdemi hozzájárulás egy olyan politikaelmélethez, amely nem ismeri félre a politika mozgásait és nem veti el őket anélkül», «Kérdéses azonban, mitől térne vissza a demokráciák önintézményesítő képessége napjainkban. Müller érezhetően kesztyűs kézzel bánik a baloldali egalitarizmussal, úgy tet szik, ennek részleges inkorporálását ajánlja amerikai olvasóinak. Bernie Sanders és társai igényeiben Müller voltaképpeni szociáldemokrata irányultságot lát, ezért nem is tekinti őket populistának.», «Müller fő meglátásait a posztszocialista populizmusok vizsgálatából meríti, ám eltekint attól, hogy Orbán vagy Kaczyński kritikája a fennálló alkotmányos rendszerekkel kapcsolatban mé lyebbre nyúlik, mint a 2008-as válság, egészen e rendszerek keletkezéséig.»

Bjørn Jespersen, Technical University of Ostrava — https://www.ceeol.com/search/viewpdf?id=706720 — «The author is openly in favour of democracy and openly against populism, but what I found appealing about the book is that it resists the temptation to speak condescendingly of populist voters, picturing them as unlettered, unwashed masses stoked up on hatred, disdain and aggression directed at everyone who is ‘them’ and not ‘us’.», «Müller ought perhaps to have spelt o ut in more detail the fact that the populist is not opposed to elites per se. First, the populists when politically successful become (part of) the elite themselves (though they would not label themselves as such, of course). Second, even when in opposition, the populists will look kindly upon those portions of the existing elites that serve the populist cause.», «This engaging monograph is a fine example of applied political philosophy. It is also exceptionally timely.»

Juan F González-Bertomeu, Instituto Tecnológico Autónomo de México, Maria Paula Saffon Universidad Nacional Autónoma de México — https://academic.oup.com/icon/article/15/4/1231/4872590 — «While the book concerns itself with populism under democratic or electoral rule, there have been many instances of non-democratic populism, many of them in Latin America (Velasco Alvarado in Peru, Somoza in Nicaragua, etc.), and some even with an allegedly left-wing leaning. Apart from the reoccurrence of elections (or lack thereof), one can legitimately ask whether there are any other differences between openly authoritarian populism and populism under electoral rule.», «The Spanish Podemos criticizes elites and at times uses a totalizing rhetoric, but is it really a populist movement on an equal footing with the likes of Erdoğan?», «The opposite risk is underinclusion. In Müller’s words, populists assume that the people issue something like an imperative mandate telling them what to do, so there really is no need for debate and participation. Yet at least some political regimes centrally identified as “populist” diverge from this picture. Again, Morales’s Bolivia is one.», «The view of populism Müller presents is a bit static, from opposition to the government and from one year to the next, when this is not necessarily so in all cases.», «None of the previous questions, we hasten to add, diminishes the great value of this book»

John Abromeit, Department of History, State University of New York, Buffalo State, Buffalo — https://www.cogitatiopress.com/politicsandgovernance/article/download/1146/1146 — «No doubt, Mudde and Kaltwasser’s approach, which makes room for progressive, bottom–up forms of populism, is more supple here. But Müller’s approach has the advantage of capturing one decisive aspect of right-wing populism that many commentators have overlooked, namely, its tendency to depoliticize its followers and to reduce democracy to a spectacle, in which passive citizens do nothing more than watch or listen to their leaders.», «But I would like briefly to discusstwo weaknesses I see in his approach, which he shareswith Mudde and Kaltwasser. The first is his positing ofliberal democracy as the unquestionable telos of modern politics.», «the question is whether or not hepossesses the conceptual tools to grasp the reasons whyliberal democracy has come increasingly under threat,from within, during the past few decades.», «Müller is too quick tocaricature and dismiss social-psychological explanationsof populism, such as Adorno and his colleagues’ analy-ses of the authoritarian personality.», «Not surprisingly, Müller is him-self explicitly critical of Laclau, yet he—like Mudde andKaltwasser—approach populism as a fundamentallypo-liticalphenomenon, and make little effort to systemat-ically explore the socio-historical and social psychologi-cal factors that have determined its success.»

[BOOK_OR_AUTHOR_OR_CONCEPT_CRITICISM] Prof. Dr. Dirk Jörke, TU Darmstadt — https://elibrary.utb.de/doi/pdf/10.3224/zpth.v7i2.04 — «Müllers Text hilft uns zu verstehen, wa-rum und in welchem Ausmaß der Populismus eine Gefahr für die liberale Demokratie darstellt, aber hilft uns leider nicht – und damit komme ich zu meinen kritischen Ausführungen – zu verstehen, wie wir dieser Gefahr begegnen können», «Jedenfalls wird von Müller zu wenig beachtet, dass sich in den vergangenen zwei, drei Jahrzehnten in Europa die politi-sche Landschaft stark verändert hat.», «Mein Unbehagen an der von Müller und so vielen anderen betriebenen politiktheoreti-schen Auseinandersetzung mit dem Populismus besteht nicht zuletzt darin, dass die Kollate-ralschäden des zeitgenössischen Liberalismus nicht reflektiert werden.», «Die Ausführungen von Michéa wie auch die von Rorty und Frank verweisen auf jene blinden Flecken eines liberalen Diskurses über den Populismus, für den der Text von Müller nur ein Beispiel unter vielen ist.»

[REVIEW_LONG] Prof. Dr. Karin Priester, emeritierte Professorin der Westfälischen Wilhelms-Universität Münster — https://elibrary.utb.de/doi/pdf/10.3224/zpth.v7i2.05 — «Bisweilen führt das bei Müller zu einer gewissen Sprunghaftigkeit, zu Abschweifungen und einseitig ausgewählten Belegen.», «Populisten, so seine Hauptthese, verstünden die politische Willensbildung als imperatives Mandat. Das bestreite ich.», «Diese These untermauert er noch mit den „Ver-trägen“, die Populisten mit dem Volk schließen. Aus der US-amerikanischen Politik dürf-te ihm aber bekannt sein, dass diese „Verträge“ in allen politischen Lagern verbreitet sind und nichts anderes als das Wahlprogramm einer Partei beinhalten. Bill Clinton versprach 1992 einen „New Covenant“, eine „feierliche Übereinkunft“ zwischen dem Volk und sei-ner Regierung. Der republikanische Politiker Newt Gingrich präsentierte sein Programm als „Contract with America“. Sind Clinton und Gingrich deswegen Populisten? Aus meiner Sicht verkennt Müller das spezifische Verhältnis von Führer und Geführ-ten im Populismus.», «Irritierend finde ich dagegen Müllers esoterische Digressionen zur Unfassbarkeit und Nicht-Darstellbarkeit des Volkes in seiner Gesamtheit, erst recht sein Dekret: „Demokra-ten müssen schlicht akzeptieren, dass das Volk als solches sich nie ganz fassen lässt“», «Leider übersieht er, dass sich auch die Gegenseite schwer tut, unliebsame Wahlergebnisse zu akzeptieren. Man erinnere sich an die Volks-abstimmungen zur EU-Verfassung in Frankreich und den Niederlanden 2005, die von der „Straße“ ins Parlament verlagert wurden, um das von der EU gewünschte Ergebnis zu er-zielen.», «Müller gebührt das Verdienst, die Debatten über Populismus wieder in demokratietheo-retische Bahnen gelenkt zu haben. Aber die Gattung des Essays verleitet auch zu einem gro-ben Pinselstrich und zu feuilletonistischem Impressionismus, etwa, wenn er mit souveräner Geste die weit verbreitete Gleichsetzung von populistischen Führern mit Charismatikern vom Tisch wischt.», «Grosso modo ist Müller auch darin zuzustimmen, dass es Populisten nicht um mehr Partizipation, sondern um Akklamation geht, auch wenn er seine Beispiele sehr selektiv auswählt. Mit Geert Wildersʼ Partij voor de Vrijheid (PVV) und Berlusconis Forza Italia hat er zwar leichtes Spiel, aber wie repräsentativ sind diese Fälle für „den“ Populismus?», «Ähnlich einseitig sind auch Müllers Ausführungen zu populistischen Herrschaftspraktiken.», «Auch Müller ist, bei allem Scharfsinn, ein Moralist, der rund siebzig Jahre nach Popper heute den Feind der offenen Gesellschaft im Populismus er-blickt. Dessen Gegner, die moralisch Guten, nennt er zwar „aufgeklärte Demokraten“, meint aber „aufgeklärte Eliten“. Müllers Hauptthese vom imperativen Mandat im Populismus halte ich für falsch. Aber er hat einen wichtigen Impuls ausgelöst, um erneut die Frage nach Sinn, Bedeutung und Reichweite von Demokratie aufzuwerfen. Über Populismus lässt sich gehaltvoll nur vor diesem Hintergrund diskutieren.»

[REVIEW_SMASHER] José Fernández Vega, Universidad de Buenos Aires — http://www.scielo.org.mx/scielo.php?script=sci_arttext&pid=S2395-86692018000400126 — «El autor rechaza fundar su caracterización en una lábil psicología política que parece inspirada en los prejuicios sobre el infantilismo emocional de las mayorías o las masas peligrosas heredados del siglo XIX. Toma distancia, asimismo, del desprecio de muchos comentaristas acerca del atraso rural y la escasa educación de una base social predominantemente masculina, si bien estas cualidades pueden manifestarse en ciertas variantes del populismo.», «Müller parece creer que, más allá de las declaraciones, las democracias de nuestro tiempo sí la promoverían, algo que su inclinación empírica podría fácilmente desmentir con la cifra de abstenciones electorales y las reiteradas alarmas por la apatía política general. Aplicada al pasado, dicha inclinación por los hechos permitiría constatar cuántos populismos se apoyaron en la actividad de las masas de un modo u otro (vale decir, liberando sus energías o controlando su despliegue).», «Según Müller, los populistas suelen confeccionar constituciones a medida de sus ambiciones y no validadas por el voto. Pero la Unión Europea ha dado ejemplos similares durante los últimos lustros por motivos que el propio Müller analiza al final de su libro y explica por las suspicacias respecto de la soberanía popular de los arquitectos de la Unión, escaldados por el pasado fascista del continente, que pretendían dejar atrás.», «La idealización de la democracia realmente existente es una debilidad del libro.», «Müller, sin embargo, considera al populismo como un producto patológico específico de las democracias representativas, cuyas “promesas incumplidas” (la referencia es a Norberto Bobbio) terminan engendrándolo. Un populismo histórico y emblemático, el de Juan Perón, invalidaría esta tesis.», «Resulta difícil compatibilizar semejante afirmación con el inexorable fiscal compact de Merkel y de su ministro Schäuble, por no hablar de la previa e indiscutible guerra al eje del mal de Bush Jr. Cuesta creer que un politólogo alemán que profesa en Princeton esté desinformado respecto de estas dos políticas que de algún modo configuraron nuestra época y, cuyos complejos efectos enardecen a las bases del populismo en su continente de origen.», «La idealización corre pareja con la demonización. Müller se respalda en ejemplos actuales. Hay escaso recurso a la historia en su ensayo, aunque allí se cite la frase de Nietzsche según la cual sólo se puede definir aquello que no tiene historia, y la del populismo es muy extensa y variada.», «El problema de Müller es que su examen deriva de una visión moralista de la democracia -sistema superior por definición-y es selectivo en sus ejemplificaciones. Su método coquetea con la sociología y la historia, pero no emprende un análisis detallado en esa dirección, sino que confronta un tipo ideal de democracia con un desfavorecido tipo real de populismo.»

Ingo Elbe, Carl von Ossietzky Universität Oldenburg — https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Ingo_Elbe/publication/326040527_Jan-Werner_Muller_Co_to_jest_populizm/links/5b34dcea0f7e9b0df5d3d815/Jan-Werner-Mueller-Co-to-jest-populizm.pdf?origin=publication_detail — «W analizie przyczyn aktualnej fali populizmu esej Müllera wypada jednak blado. Również jego re-cepty na poradzenie sobie z problemami, w swoisty sposób podejmowanymi i artykułowanymi przez populistów, pozostają na poziomie zwykłego moralizowania i przeoczają płynną granicę między nacjo-nalizmem tradycyjnych partii a populistycznymi dyskursami dyskryminacyjnymi», «Nie przeczę, że populistyczne ruchy konstruują opisywaną przez Müllera homogeniczną wolę narodu, którą ostatecznie wykorzystują do legitymacji swojej elitarystycznej i dyk-tatorskiej polityki. Jednakże pojęcie „antypluralizm” więcej zaciemnia niż rozjaśnia, gdy już samo, mające pozytywne konotacje, przeciwstawne pojęcie „pluralizm” skrywa wrzucone do jednego worka określone socjoekonomiczne antagonistyczne interesy oraz zwykłą różnorodność interesów», «Perspektywa czysto semantyczna i instytucjo-nalna (s. 65, 90 [wyd. niem.])10, jak również mglisty, a nawet wypaczony obraz podejścia psychologii społecznej do problemu populizmu (s. 35-36)11 prowadzą do nadwyżki części opisowej w jego analizie. Müller nie sili się nawet na wyjaśnienie fenomenu u jego podstaw.», «Przedstawienie parlamentarno-demokratycznych procesów pozostaje u Müllera bez oparcia w postaci teorii społecznej.»

Sławomir Drelich, Uniwersytet Mikołaja Kopernika w Toruniu ( https://www.wnopib.umk.pl/katedra-mysli-politycznej-2/pracownicy/dr-slawomir-drelich/ ) — http://cejsh.icm.edu.pl/cejsh/element/bwmeta1.element.desklight-06748748-49be-49e3-958c-0cbc4afd6dee/c/Slawomir_Drelich.pdf — «I rzeczywiście zapro-ponowane przez autora differentia specifica populizmu zdaje się byćtyleż ogólne, co mało przekony-wujące w świetle dotychczasowych badań nad populizmem.», «Rozczarowu-jące jest, iż autor rozważania swoje opiera na dość wybiórczo dobranej literaturze przedmiotu ichociażznaleźć można odwołania do prac Ernesta Gellnera, Ghity Ionescu, Benjamina Arditiego, Michaela Kazina czy Richarda Hofstadtera, to jednak brakuje odniesień do konkluzji ianaliz uznanych na całym świecie politologów zajmu-jących się populizmem, których prace stanowią swoisty kanon dla współczesnych badaczy tego zja-wiska. Odnieść można wrażenie, że literatura przedmiotu dobrana została wtaki sposób, aby oprzećkontrowersyjne niekiedy propozycje Müllera na wybranych celowo autorytetach świata akademickiego.», «Niestety również Müller – pomimo zamie-rzeń – ulega tej słabości. Tak jest bowiem zprzykładami przywo-ływanymi przez autora, zaś jego postawa – dostrzegalna chociażby wtrzecim rozdziale zatytułowanym Jak sobie radzić zpopulistami? –także zdaje się być skażona swo-istym lękiem przed współczesnymi populistami, który raczej nie powi-nien być manifestowany wnauko-wej pracy politologicznej.», «Müller twierdzi, że „nie może byćpopulizmu bez kogoś, kto przema-wiałby wimieniu narodu jako cało-ści” (s.41), tymczasem przyjęcie takiego założenia zmuszałoby nas do uznania, że wdobie demokracji parlamentarnej każdy polityk wal-czący o masowe poparcie jest nolens volens populistą.», «Tak widzący wspólnotę narodową (czy też lud) populiści – zdaniem autora – prze-konują, że „istnieje coś takiego jak jedno wspólne dobro, które naród jest wstanie rozpoznać iktórego pragnie” (s.47). Wydaje się jednak, że jest to jedna zcech typowych dla masowych partii politycznych działających wpaństwach demo-kratycznych, natomiast sama idea „dobra wspólnego” – posiadająca de facto źródła wklasycznej koncepcji polityki», «Ponadto Müller podkreśla, że „partie populistyczne mają szcze-gólną predylekcję do wewnętrz-nego autorytaryzmu” (s. 62), co jednakże nie do końca zgadza sięzdotychczasowymi ustaleniami badaczy populizmu, wskazującymi na istnienie zarówno autorytarnej wersji populizmu (typowej cho-ciażby dla nurtów latynoamery-kańskich), jak również jego wersji demokratycznej (indyjski gandyzm czy też polska tzw. Pierwsza Soli-darność)», «Trudno zgodzić się zprzekona-niem autora, iż wszystkie te cechy zawsze stanowić będą wyznaczniki populizmu – bardziej należałoby wiązać je zautorytaryzmem sensu stricto aniżeli zpopulizmem», «Wydaje się, że także wtym miejscu konkluzje Müllera zdają się abstrahować od faktu, iżpolitologom ihistorykom wsamym XXwieku udało się opisać różne wersje populizmu: bardziej demo-kratyczne ibardziej autorytarne; także takie, które wmniejszym lub większym stopniu podporząd-kowywały się ustrojowo-prawnemu status quo.», «Niezależnie od nieścisłości, cza-sami również sprzeczności, atakże nieuprawnionych generalizacji, książka Müllera słusznie podnosi coś, na co zwracali uwagę wszyscy dotychczasowi badacze populizmu, amianowicie na fakt, iż jednym zcelów populistów – wkażdym razie na poziomie deklaratywnym – jest chęć „dowartościowania tych części społeczeństwa, które dotych-czas były wykluczone”», «Większość bada-czy sugeruje jednak, że populizm nie jest nurtem ani prawicowym, ani lewicowym – jeśli mówić o nim jako o doktrynie politycznej czy ideologii (choć ico do tego nie ma zgody), wówczas należy przy-znać, że stanowi nurt eklektyczny», «Jego propozycja jednakże zdaje się być przy-najmniej niedopracowana iwielokrotnie abstrahować od klasycznych refleksji na temat populizmu. Największą warto-ścią jego pracy jest fakt, iż stara się on oprzeć ją na szeregu współczesnych przykładach, szczególnie zaś na przy-kładach europejskich.»

Emile Chabal, University of Edinburgh — https://sci-hub.se/10.1080/17496977.2017.1348026 — «The second chapter deals with what populists do once they are in power. Müller’s analysis isless clear-cut here.», «Finally, in the third chapter, Müller tries to offer a template for how to deal withpopulism. This is even less coherent than the second chapter.», «In the twenty-first century, it is rarely enough for populists simply to claim theyspeak for the people; the people must believe them too. So, while Müller offers a powerfuland persuasive framework for understanding the function of populism, he is less good atexplaining its recent successes. If nothing else, closer attention to the content of populist ideol-ogies would have reminded him that populism in contemporary democracies always dependson a fickle collusion between populist leaders and the fantasies of the people they claim to represent»

Nirupam Hazra, Bankura University — https://sci-hub.se/10.1080/14662043.2018.1516528 — «Müller believes properargument and evidence can make a difference and create a dent in populistsupport base. He illustrates this claim by referring to George Wallace’s 1968 pre-sidential campaign. But Müller does not show how effective it is in the current pol-itical context. Can a populist be countered with proper arguments and evidence ina post-truth world where truth has increasingly lost its relevance? In a world wherefacts are fudged and truths are manufactured, it will not be easy to challenge thepopulists with correct statistics», «Müller’s analysis of populism provides a refreshingly new dimension to theunderstanding of the phenomenon, but what still may trouble some of thereaders is the rise of populist leaders to power across the world. Müller fails toexplain this rise»

[REVIEW_LONG][REVIEW_SMASHER][REVIEW_HIGH_ERUDITION] Yannis Stavrakakis, Aristotle University of Thessaloniki, Thessaloniki, Greece; Anton Jager, University of Cambridge, Cambridge, United Kingdom — https://sci-hub.se/10.1177/1368431017723337 — «Especially since Mu ̈ller seems to ignore or downplay the importanceof previous theorizations of the phenomenon», «What Is Populism? reads more like a polemical pamphlet in the tradition of militant democracy (wehrhafteorstreitbare Demokratie) than a critical investigation.», «In a rather predictable way, having painted such a one-sided rendering of the phenomenon, Muller spends a fair chunk of his book orchestrating the liberal defences against its onslaught», «In opposition to Muller’s largely ahistorical and excessively normative», «Indeed, Mudde and Kaltwasserhere exhibit a clear understanding of the differences between the liberal and the democratic tradition, which allows them to avoid the largely a-historical equation between democracy and liberalism so ubiquitous in Muller», «in Muller’s passionless, numerically objective, liberaldystopia», «Muller seems to reduce human subjectivity to the most banal and rationalistic individualism, ignoring the symbolic and imaginary constitution of human reality as well as the crucial role affect, emotion, and passion play in socio-political life.», «Second, and mostimportant given the discredited status of its original formulation (see, for a detailedanalysis, Ja ̈ger, 2016; Stavrakakis, 2017), they place doubt on the plausibility of thiscriterion, which should be urgently reconsidered from scratch.», «Yet, the crucial problem with the criterion of moralization is not its origins and/or itsdubious intellectual trajectory; it is its precise status as one of the minimal criteria forthe differential identification of populism. Indeed, one is left wondering what such acriterion really means and how it could be effectively deployed.», «It is difficult, in other words, to substantiate an exclusive link of exaggerated orpathological types of moralization to populism.», «In Muller’s world, itis mainly populists who engage in the politics of fantasy – all the others seem to stick toreality and evidence-based politics.», «The accomplishments of the new mainstream in populismresearch, signified by these two interventions, will undoubtedly help contemporarycommentators get closer to a more adequate understanding of the complex creaturecurrently lying under their microscope. At the same time, their limitations will highlightthe fact that, as in Mary Shelley’s famed novella, this creature is very often constructed –at least partly – in line with the theoretico-political stereotypes of this last incarnation ofthe ‘modern Prometheus’, the populism researcher.»

<a id="Учебные-пособия-1"></a>
### Учебные пособия

<!--- [ACADEMIC_DEGREE] заведующая кафедрой Кафедра политической теории; научный руководитель образовательных программ, старший научный сотрудник Кафедра регионального управления и национальной политики; Кандидат исторических наук, доктор философских наук. Член Ученых советов по политологии и социологии МГИМО, МГУ и Института философии РАН. — https://mgimo.ru/people/alekseeva/

[ACADEMIC_DEGREE_EDITORS] Марина Михайловна Лебедева — «Профессор, доктор политических наук, кандидат психологических наук» — https://mgimo.ru/people/lebedeva-mm/ ; Мария Михайловна Фёдорова — «Кандидат философских (1983 г.) и доктор политических наук (2005 г.). С 2005 г. возглавляет сектор истории политической философии.» — https://iphras.ru/page17274613.htm

[POSITIVE_OR_NEUTRAL_REVIEW][REVIEW_LONG] Спиридонова Валерия Игоревна, Владимир николаевич Шевченко — институт философии РАН — http://vphil.ru/index.php?option=com_content&task=view&id=1387 — «Книги Т.А. Алексеевой пользуются повышенным вниманием, в них каждый раз весьма удачно соединяются исследовательское и преподавательское начала. Глубокое знание огромного количества источников вместе с простотой и доступностью изложения делают тексты книг привлекательными для чтения.», «Несомненной удачей автора можно назвать анализ взглядов Лео Штрауса, крупнейшего американского политического мыслителя XX в. Обращает на себя внимание четкое изложение того вызова, который Л. Штраус бросил американской университетской науке.», «В разделе «Идеология как ‟политическое воображаемое”» Т.А. Алексеевой удалось высказать, пожалуй, всё самое важное, относящееся к проблеме идеологии. Автор подчеркивает, что единого, в смысле общепринятого, определения идеологии не существует, причем многие из них противоречат друг другу.», «Несомненным плюсом автора данного учебного пособия является логически ясное и максимально простое изложение очень сложных вопросов.», «При этом нужно заметить, что, несмотря на определенную занимательность изложения, автору удается указать на все главные повороты обсуждаемого сюжета.», «В целом следует сказать, что Т.А. Алексеева, принимаясь за решение достаточно сложного вопроса – изложить доступно и одновременно максимально полно относительно новый дискурс современности – политическую теорию в связи со становлением теории международных отношений, успешно справилась с поставленной задачей. Автору удалось создать четкое и объемное представление о развитии политической теории в целом, которая к концу XX в. распространила свое методологическое влияние на такую специфическую и прагматическую область, какой всегда были международные отношения. Вместе с тем автор этого нового, не только учебного, но и без сомнения, значимого научного труда сумел наглядно показать и доказать, что интеграция политической теории и теории международных отношений в единую дисциплину стала научным фактом, и потому новая книга Т.А. Алексеевой несомненно станет значимым событием в отечественной политической мысли.»

[Алмонд Габриэль Абрахам](https://www.britannica.com/biography/Gabriel-Almond), [Бинем Пауэлл Дж.](https://www.sas.rochester.edu/psc/people/view.php?fid=4), [Стром Кааре](https://polisci.ucsd.edu/people/faculty/faculty-directory/currently-active-faculty/strom-profile.html), [Далтон Рассел](https://www.socsci.uci.edu/~rdalton/) — Сравнительная политология сегодня. Thomas Kikauer, Catherine Link, Western Sydney University — https://sci-hub.se/10.1111/awr.12205

Onze onderzoeksresultaten suggereren alvast dat er op dit niveau heel wat mogelijkheden openliggen.»

Nobody will contemplate it.Graebermust be aware of these Keynes-style arguments.», «Since the economyalready always tends toward stagnation because the insufficiency of the inducement toinvest has already always been a bottleneck economic problem, the disappearance of bullshitjobs would be too awful to contemplate. Nobody will contemplate it.»

Graeber estime que le phénomène des « bullshit jobs » est d’une ampleur considérable, mais ne peut s’appuyer que sur un sondage de taille limitée réalisé par l’institut YouGov UK, d’après lequel 37 % des répondants estiment que leur travail n’apporte pas "une contribution significative au monde"», «Le sentiment d’inutilité et d’ennui ne concerne donc pas que des emplois qualifiés : les témoignages de l’ouvrage reflètent un biais vers les professions intellectuelles.», «Stimulant et souvent amusant, le livre de D. Graeber souffre néanmoins d’un trop faible ancrage dans les sciences du travail, qui l’empêche d’avancer vers des pistes crédibles de solutions.», «L’absence de références aux sciences du travail contribue sans doute à expliquer la faiblesse des propositions avancées par D. Graeber pour remédier à la situation, et qui se résument en fait à l’instauration d’un revenu de base.», «Mais, plus fondamentalement, en quoi le revenu de base permettrait-il de faire reculer les "bullshit jobs"»

Damit wider-spricht er nicht nur mit der eigenen Argumentation, denn wenn eine Tätigkeittatsächlich völlig sinnlos wäre, so würde auch deren Automatisierung keinenSinn machen.»

1. Zweig David — Invisibles. The Power of Anonymous Work in an Age of Relentless Self-Promotion (Portfolio, 2014).epub
<!--- [JOURNALISM_DEGREE] «Terkel’s Pulitzer Prize-winning The Good War (1984)» — https://www.britannica.com/biography/Studs-Terkel

[POSITIVE_OR_NEUTRAL_REVIEW] Leon Fink, University of Illinois at Chicago — https://citeseerx.ist.psu.edu/viewdoc/download?doi=10.1.1.995.7840&rep=rep1&type=pdf — «Studs Terkel’s Working: People Talk about What They Do All Day and HowThey Feel About What They Do has attained something of an iconic statussince its original publication in 1974.», «Of course, setting Working’s author in the context of his times hardlyexhausts the value of the work itself. The interviews remain to this day aninvaluable, and unpredictable, repository of descriptions of work environmentsand the thoughts of those who occupied them», «Yet, with the possible exception of Barbara Ehrenreich (2001, 2008), no otherwriter has succeeded in placing the voices of working Americans at the centreof compelling, popular expositions of the national mood.»

[REVIEW_LONG][REVIEW_HIGH_ERUDITION] Dorothy Deering — https://sci-hub.se/https://www.jstor.org/stable/27796563 — «Sociologists have complained that Terkel has not followed ap proved sampling procedures and therefore that Terkel' s approach is impressionistic rather than scientific. Who could duplicate his results? they ask. Oral historians have joined the sociologists in faulting the book for its lack of analysis and explanation. In dismay they wail, "Terkel allows himself the freedom of a novelist in selecting material." Precisely. Terkel makes no claims to have written a scientific sociological or historical study. His claim is far greater. He has enabled people to express themselves in their unique humanity.», «Terkel's work gains enormously in the integrity we can see it grants the worker, for it lacks any hint of the condescending tone that pervades Lasson's book», « As egalitarian history these interviews confirm the actual and potential presence of a self-conscious and articulate work-force (still largely unrecognized and untapped) that has waited for and found its historian in Studs Terkel.»

Gus Tyler, Assistant President International Ladies' Garment Workers' Union, New York, 1975 — https://sci-hub.se/10.2307/2521464 — «Terkel allows wide latitude to his subjects. They become people first and "workers" second. Through their eyes-not Terkel's-the reader is allowed to peek at worlds he has never seen or even been aware of.», « Despite Terkel's obvious dedication to objectivity (let them say it like it is), the collection may not be as unbiased as the author himself wishes. A piece of Terkel enters the work when he makes his decisions of whom to interview. The silent ones make poor copy; the articulate ones with strong minds are more likely to grab the reader», «Terkel hints at his own bias in the opening lines of his introduction», « In all, "working"-the thing and the book-is many-sided, many-sorrowed, and many-splendored»

Anthony G. Porreca, University of Tennessee — https://sci-hub.se/10.1177/074171367402500107 — «The frustrations and unhappinesses that exist among many workersare the most astonishing, if not disturbing, content found in the book.», «This broad-based approachto workers’ attitudes toward work is more meaningful than a basic re-port of worker attitudes in isolated occupations. The commonalities thatexist among workers in America are the key factors that make Workinga valuable adult education resource.», «The timely contribution of the book is significant, for it recordsAmerican workers’ view of their jobs as a chore, as a daily humiliation,and as an occasional joy. Perhaps this book will initiate a serious searchfor improved working and living conditions, which, of course, must beinitiated within ourselves.»

Berenice M. Fisher, New York University — https://sci-hub.se/https://www.jstor.org/stable/367849 — «Working, has already received a good deal of attention, in part due to the indictment of our vocational (and social) life it seems to imply. Yet, the book's message is far from unambiguous. The over one-hundred interview statements are filled with complaints about work-its boredom, its physical pain, its degradation-but the range and density of the material is great enough to support a wide variety of theories about the meaning of work.»

[BOOK_OR_AUTHOR_OR_CONCEPT_CRITICISM] Lucie Kučerová (возможно — https://www.slu.cz/fpf/cz/ustav-cizich-jazyku/lide/lucie-kucerova/ ), 2011 — https://journals.muni.cz/discourse-and-interaction/article/download/6964/8507 — «As illustrated on several examples from Hard Times: An Oral History of the Great Depression, these procedures signifi cantly altered the form of the original utterances of the interviewees, which prompts the question of who the author of the texts really is.», «The comparison of the original interview transcripts and their edited versions reveals that the interviewees’ utterances were at places altered to such an extent that it becomes questionable who the author of the utterances really is.», «He is not only appreciated for having let the voices of numerous “etceteras” (Terkel 2007: XV) be heard, but also for his talent to make people open up and talk about things they had never talked about or feelings they never knew they felt.», «The biggest difference can be seen between Dorothe’s interview, which was shortened almost 10.5 times, and the interview with Frank and Rome Hentges, where the UT is only 2.5 times shorter than the ET.», «Such cuts obviously infl uenced not only the way the speaker seems to express herself (less hesitation and uncertainty, shorter sentences)», «also obtain a text in which any given passage might have been reorganized or re-sequenced in a way entirely dependent on Studs Terkel’s idea of the form that the text should have», «As example (4) demonstrates, however, Studs Terkel makes changes even in cases where no correction was necessary», «Since Terkel’s books are generally regarded as containing the voices of hundreds of Americans, the paper aimed at drawing attention to the fact that the interviewees’ utterances underwent considerable alterations which were motivated by Terkel’s attempt to offer something very specifi c to his readership.»

## Самопомощь

<!--- [ACADEMIC_DEGREE] «PhD, Research Professor: Emeritus Distinguished Professor, Cognitive Science», «Studying choice and decision-making in humans and non-humans with the aim of understanding the psychological and economic basis of self-control, addiction, social cooperation, and altruism.» — https://www.stonybrook.edu/commcms/psychology/faculty/faculty_profiles/hrachlin

[POSITIVE_OR_NEUTRAL_REVIEW] Edmund Fantino and Stephanie Stolarz-Fantino — https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC1284891/pdf/jeabehav007800100117.pdf — «Although we take some issue with teleolog-ical behaviorism, the theory of behavior advocated by Rachlin, we recommend this book to anyoneinterested in self-control.», «From the standpointof evaluating a book as a useful textbook fora seminar, it is far more important that thebook inspires intelligent and heated discus-sion than that it inspires total agreement.», «Despite the applied implications of temporally extended response patterning, this is avowedly not a ‘‘self-help’’ book, as Rachlintakes pains to state in his Introduction. Actual methods of instituting behavioral patterningto enhance self-control and monitoring one’sadherence to these patterns are not emphasized.», «For example, Rachlinequates commitment with a reduction in freedom, an equation that we believe holds in only a narrow sense.», «Rachlin was among the first investigators of self-control to recognize it as a special case ofchoice (immediate small reward vs. a largerdelayed reward) and to point out that behav-ior involving self-control must therefore obey the normal laws of choice (e.g., Rachlin&Green, 1972). It is not surprising that a com-prehensive discussion of self-control inevitably involves discussion of some general principles of behavior.», «In any event, Rachlin is surely correct thatpersistent behavior often assists us in achiev-ing our goals; this, in turn, most likely con-tributes to sunk-cost errors.», «In all of these cases, although thebroad parallels are appreciated, the extent ofthe concordance, particularly when quantita-tive theories are involved, is by no meansagreed on», «Rachlin’s treatment of gambling is one ofthe high points of his insightful book.», «A potential problem with Rachlin’s presentation of teleological behav-iorism is its apparently unabashedly goal-directed character. In this book Rachlin does not make clear the extent to which the emphasis on final cause (as exemplified by his remarks quoted above, about the cash at the cash machine) depends on consequences (the final cause) previously experienced.», «In our view, the powerfuland intriguing analysis of self-control pre-sented inThe Science of Self-Controlhas broadapplicability, whether or not we accept the au-thor’s view of teleological behaviorism. Thisis indeed “a good read.”»

<a id="HardCriticism-6"></a>
#### HardCriticism

<!--- [ACADEMIC_DEGREE] «PhD, University of California, Los Angeles; Research Interests Philosophy of Psychology» — https://www.philosophy.ucsb.edu/people/herbert-fingarette

[POSITIVE_OR_NEUTRAL_REVIEW][REVIEW_ONE_PAGE] David R. Rudy, Morehead State University — https://sci-hub.se/10.2307/2073887 — «Fingarette has produced an outstanding work, not because it is the definitive treatment on heavy drinking but because it is a sound, rational, thought-provoking treatment of much of the contemporary American alcoholism enterprise. It will remain a valuable contribution to the literature on drinking behavior for a long time.»

[REVIEW_ONE_PAGE] Paul Schmolling, Ph.D. Mental Health & Human Services Program Kingsborough Community College City University of New York Brooklyn — https://sci-hub.se/https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/abs/pii/0740547289900536 — «This book is a model of effective writing for the general reader about a specialized field. Regretably, books written for professionals rarely attain the sharp, incisive style of this one.», «In summary, this is a compact, well-argued book for the general reader which presents a powerful critique of the disease model of alcoholism.»

[REVIEW_HIGH_ERUDITION] M. M. Glatt, Huntercombe Manor Hospital, Huntercombe Lane South, Taplow, Maidenhead, Berks — https://sci-hub.se/10.1093/oxfordjournals.alcalc.a045151 — «Hegoes out of his way to attack the 'discredited'Classic Disease Concept of alcoholism, 'itstenets and beliefs contradicted and refuted bydecades of scientific research'», «It is obvious that the disease concept ofalcoholism, put forth by Jelliiik and funda-mental to the teaching of AA, so stronglycriticized by Fingarette, did not apply to allheavy drinking as Jellinek (1960) himself tookpains to stress: defining alcoholism broadly as'any drinking that causes any damage'», «The question ofwhether mild or moderately dependent drink-ers can practise controlled drinking may indeedbe controversial, but in the case of severelydependent drinkers, a recent inquiry in theBritish Journal of Addictions (1986, 1987)showed a fairly uniform agreement on the needfor total abstinence», «although one may doubt whether this approach would be advised for the severely dependent drinker», «Professor Fingarette's book is well resear-ched, written in a lucid style, highly informa-tive and often provocative. His tendency to avoid the term 'alcohol dependence' and toreplace it with 'heavy drinking' often makes forsemantic difficulties and confusion.»

Ferdinand Schoeman, University of South Carolina, Columbia — https://sci-hub.se/https://www.jstor.org/stable/2185080 — «Heavy Drinking is an elegant, engaging, and synoptic treatment of a most perplexing set of issues relating to long-term alcohol abuse, especially the kind of issue the Court faced in Traynor», «I do not think that he regards the demolition of the "classic" disease concept of alcoholism and his profoundly insightful reanalysis of long-term drinking patterns as meaningful and selected as settling irrebuttably an individual's accountability for his/her excessive drinking patterns. The contours and complexities of individual life histories are too tangled and variable for such a presumption.»

[REVIEW_SEMI] Anders Bergmark, Stockholm University ( https://www.su.se/english/profiles/anber-1.182799 ); Lars Oscarsson, Ersta Sköndal University College ( https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Lars_Oscarsson ) — https://journals.sagepub.com/doi/pdf/10.1177/145507258900600217 — «Denna bakgrund, en blandning av distans och insiderposition, gor Fingarette til! en i hogsta grad lamp-lig person att kommentera klyftan mellan populariserade myter och ve-tenskapliga fakta.», «Nar Fingarette till slut dristar sig till att ange några riktlinjer får hur behandlingen av alkoholproblem bor utvecklas uppvisar hans framstall-ning, får fårsta och enda gången, en mindre overtygande uppbyggnad.», «I sin diskussion av fciregivna och faktiska behandlings effekter presen-terar Fingarette in te bara massivite-ten hos de fakta som satter aUvarliga frågetecken infcir legitimiteten hos ett behandlings perspektiv på alko-holproblem. Han visar också på de ekonomiska omstandigheter som har en mytologireproducerande funk-tion.», ««Åven om vi som lasare blir fårsakra-de om att en behandlingsinsats mås-te ta sin utgångspunkt i den specifi-ka meningsstruktur som omgardar varje individs drickande och att de fårslag Fingarette ger ar grundade på optimism snarare an fakta, så in-finner sig en vis s tveksamhet. Plots-ligt uppvisar Fingarette en sorts pragmatism och rekommenderar t.ex. beteendeterapeutiska strategier som om det inte fanns en koppling mellan den typen av åtgarder och de artikulerade teoretiska anspråk som inlarningsteoretiker får fram», «Trots denna mindre skonhetsflack består emellertid det totaia intrycket av Fingarettes framstallning orub-bat; "Heavy Drinking" ar en snudd på idealisk popularvetenskaplig pro-dukt, åtminstone utifrån en veten-skaplig bedomningshorisont.» «Vid en bedomning ur ett "konsumentper-spektiv" ar det fårstås mojligt att bokens popularvetenskapliga mis-sion passar illa med dess budskap: Vilka, utanfår en vetenskaplig krets, ar intresserade av att bli overtygade om att alkohol is m inte ar en sjukdom?»

[BOOK_OR_AUTHOR_OR_CONCEPT_CRITICISM][REVIEW_SEMI] Craig R. Janes — Department of Anthropology and Sociology, University of Colorado at Denver — https://sci-hub.se/10.1525/maq.1990.4.4.02a00180 — «In a well organized and logical argument employing a selective but reasonably representative review of the salient literature, Fingarette concludes that a single, identifiable syndrome of alcoholic drinking does not exist», «Although to the knowledgeable reader none of this analysis is particularly new or groundbreaking, Fingarette does a good job of distilling the major elements of what is a complex sociohistorical, political, economic, and cultural problem», «Unlike part one, which is by and large an empirically sound, well-crafted, and persuasive argument, part two is prone to ill-founded speculation, and what one suspects is Fingarette's personal opinion about heavy drinkers in general.», «Given Fingarette's argument in part one that contextual factors are powerfully influential in drinking behavior, his emphasis on highly individualized treatment strategies that stress "personal responsibility" emerges as a non sequitur. After very brief mention, those factors that in fact "shape" life-styles—culture and ethnicity, social relations, class, occupation, gender, are left by Fingarette in the shadowy background. Anthropologists will find this a frustrating and unillummating discussion.», «Fingarette may further damage his argument—particularly for nonspecialist readers—by repudiating the widely held view that one of the primary goals of treatment should be total abstinence.», «However, it seems counterintuitive to suggest that simply helping a person reduce his consumption to moderate levels, rather than helping a person to achieve complete abstinence, will generate the kind of fundamental life-style change that Fingarette argues must be the primary goal bf treatment.», «This approach parallels current work in the prevention field and highlights the major political and policy issues that surround alcohol availability. However, as with the discussion of treatment, Fingarette avoids discussion of the prevention implications of those messy "intervening" social variables that affect alcohol consumption: the value or function drinking in particular subcultural contexts (ethnic groups, neighborhoods, families, and occupations) and how and why such values and functions develop, as well as the social processes that may give rise to or shape the particular contexts in which individuals fashion their lives and thereby integrate drinking into them.», «Although the book is written for a lay audience, Fingarette's capable handling of the material and his clear and thoughtful exposition of issues relating to the cultural construction of alcoholism and alcoholism treatment offer much of interest to addiction specialists, medical social scientists, and teachers. Alcohol specialists and medical social scientists will appreciate, though perhaps not agree with, Fingarette's distillations of major research findings and his examination of these findings in the context of treatment and prevention policy. Probably the primary usefulness of the book, though, is pedagogical. It would be a good supplementary text for undergraduate courses in medicat anthropology or comparative health systems.»

[REVIEW_ONE_PAGE] Michael Moore, University of California, Berkeley, and University of Southern California — https://sci-hub.se/10.1086/293115 — «This is a courageous book. It is certain to bring down a rain of familiar criticism on its author, such as that he is no more sophisticated than Nancy Reagan on these matters, thinking that alcoholics can "just say no" to alcohol; that he will undo the work of generations in getting alcoholics accepted as sick rather than bad; etc. Yet at this level the book is immune to criticism. For its major point is surely correct: heavy drinking is a chosen pattern of behavior for which the drinker is responsible.», «To a philosophical audience the book will be disappointing, not for its conclusions but for the depth of its arguments. Complex philosophical conundrums such as the nature of disease or the nature and moral relevance of compelling cravings are not analyzed so much as treated as matters resolvable by scientific research.», «Yet as Fingarette's early work clearly evidences, there can be no scientific findings about "loss of control" and like matters without a philosophical elucidation of items such as will, compulsion, and character, and their relation to responsibility. And this the book does not provide.»

[REVIEW_ONE_PAGE][REVIEW_SMASHER] Theodore Ernst, Bethany Center Honesdale, PA — https://sci-hub.se/10.1093/sw/34.2.173 — «In posing a challenge to the Jellinek disease model, Fingarette is beating a dead horse.», «Fingarette emphasizes the fact that an etiology of alcoholism has never been established. However, known causation has never been a necessary condition for designating a morbid physical condition as a disease. Like many other diseases, the etiology of alcoholism is both unclear and complex.», «Fingarette is challenging a disease model that is no longer accepted by either clinicians or researchers.»

[REVIEW_ONE_PAGE] Marc Keller, Brookline, Mass. — https://sci-hub.se/10.15288/jsa.1990.51.86 — «To confirm his thesis, Professor Fingarette vigorously, and often with sound argument, attacks the "classic disease concept of alcoholism" which is described according to Martin Mann, and is blamed, with some justification, on E.M. Jellinek and Alcoholics Anonymous. Earlier conceptions, going back to antiquity--the real classics--are ignored. For his own nondisease concept, Fingarette relies chiefly on the work of Pattison, Sobell and Sobell (1977). He notes, again with some justification, that "no scientific research team has ever identified a biological cause that makes people chronic heavy drinkers." He has chosen to disregard the neurobehavioral disease model of Frawley (1987) and the strictly biological disease model of Kissin (1983), to cite just two examples», «True, he can argue that neither of these models has been proven by a "scientific research team," but has any scientific research team ever definitively demonstrated that schizophrenia or focal cortical seizures have a "biological cause"?», «Clearly, the professor's tactics are calculated to argue his case», «One aspect of the problem of "alcoholics' or "heavy drinkers" overlooked by Professor Fingarette was brilliantly highlighted by Selden Bacon (1958), who observed that "alcoholics do not drink" at all, they injest alcohol.»

[REVIEW_SMASHER] J. Angelo Corlett, Department of Philosophy, University of Arizona — https://sci-hub.se/https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/BF00489833 — «In analyzing Fingarette's argument for the self-control theory of drinking disorders I conclude that it is problematic for the following reasons: (1) his argument assumes that the identification of a single cause of alcoholism is a necessary condition of its being a disease; (2) unless it is already assumed (a priori) that persons with drinking disorders possess freedom and self-control to the extent that Fingarette assumes they do, then such persons are likely to suffer from apathy or defeatism regarding their condition; (3) even if Fingarette is correct in his criticism of certain health care programs for those with ssess freedom and self-control to the extent that Fingarette assumes they do, then such persons are likely to suffer from apathy or defeatism regarding their condition; (4) Fingarette's claim that those with drinking disorders are morally responsible for their actions that result from their disorders is problematic, that is, unless it can be shown that such persons act freely; and (5) Fingarette attempts to suppor/the self-control theory of alcoholism by refuting a 'straw man' conception of the disease model of alcoholism.», «Fingarette's argument contains some logical and conceptual confusions.», «If this criticism holds, then Fingarette does nothing to provide philosophical grounding for his claim that alcoholism as a disease is a myth. For his thesis rests on the disease theories of alcoholism being refuted by his argumentation.», «And if Fingarette replies that one must assume that the self-control theory is true, then he has a viciously circular argument, one which assumes from the start what it tries to conclude and is uninformative», «Even if it is the case that the disease model of alcoholism leads to apathy, and even if it is true that there is no reason to suppose that the self-control model fails to lead to apathy, it still does not follow that the disease model is wrong or that the self-control theory is correct. In fact, the apathy of patients is quite irrelevant to the matter of whether or not alcoholism is a disease», «Certainly the disease theorists of alcoholism do not have to claim (and to my knowledge in fact do not claim) that the treatability of alcoholism is a condition (of any kind) of alcoholism's being a disease. Again, Fingarette is attempting to refute a 'straw man'.», «Thus this very same criticism comes back to haunt Fingarette's self-control theory. For he has done nothing to justify his theory, even if his criticisms of competing theories holds.», «Some of the previous difficulties with Fingarette's project might be the result of yet another problem: his attempt to refute the disease theories of alcoholism by using a caricature or naive version of what is nowadays usually thought by reputable persons to be the disease concept of alcoholism.», «Fingarette is aware that "no leading research authorities accept the classic disease concept" ([1], p. 3). If this is the case, then why spend one's time refuting what no 'authority' believes? And, if Fingarette refutes this older notion of the disease concept of alcoholism in order to say what is wrong with current theories of this sort, then it is absolutely imperative that he specify the ways in which contemporary disease theories fall prey to the same errors that the classic theory does. If he fails on this count, then he clearly refutes a 'straw man'.»

Steffen Häfner Medizinische Universitätsklinik und Poliklinik — https://www.balintgesellschaft.de/ueber-die-dbg/publikationen/neuerscheinungen/rezensionen-michael-p-leiter-christina-maslach-burnout-erfolgreich-vermeiden-sechs-strategien-wie-sie-ihr-verhaeltnis-zur-arbeit-verbessern/ — «Anschauliche Fallbeispiele illustrieren die theoretischen Abschnitte. Sie sind realistisch, zeigen, dass sich einiges verändern lässt, wenn auch oft nicht alles, es aber gelingen kann, für beide Seiten ein größeres Maß an Zufriedenheit zu erzielen, mithin win-win-Situationen zu schaffen und aus negativen Verhaltenszirkeln herauszukommen. Leider fehlen Angaben, in wie weit die vorgeschlagene Vorgehensweisen nach wissenschaftlichen Kriterien sinnvoll sind.»

#### Неавторитетные источники

<!--- [NO_DEGREE]

[POSITIVE_OR_NEUTRAL_REVIEW][GOOD_POSITIVE_REVIEW] Francis Heylighen, a Professor at the Free University of Brussels, Clement Vidalis a research assistant in the ECCO group at the Free University of Brussels — https://sci-hub.se/https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S0024630108000848 — “When (or even whether) these opportunities are followedup depends more on the constraints of the current situation than on any predetermined plans. Re-ferring to plenty of personal experience, GTD users claim this method minimizes stress, while en-suring that work proceeds smoothly towards maximum productivity.”, “First, the methodminimizes the burden on memory and reasoning by systematically exploiting external memories,which (Allen argues) reduces the anxiety caused by not being sure that you remember everythingyou need to remember. Second, and more fundamentally, the consistent application of GTDshould promote all the features that characterize what Csikszentmihalyi has called the ‘flow’ state:a clear sense of purpose; regular feedback as to-dos are ‘ticked off’ one by one; on-going, unre-strained advance towards goals; and challenges (tasks) adapted to skills (personal abilities) andenvironmental circumstances (affordances).”, “The philosophy underlying GTD is that true produc-tivity should be measured not by the number ofplanned objectivesthat are achieved, but by thenumber ofintrinsically worthwhile results. Whether the results achieved are what was foreseen ornot is irrelevant to their ultimate value: what counts is the total amount of progress made.”

Bach. Kelly Marlith Flores Escudero, Bach. Mirian Noemi Vega Burgos, Universidad Privada del Norte — https://repositorio.upn.edu.pe/bitstream/handle/11537/14964/Flores%20Escudero%20Kelly%20Marlith%20-%20Vega%20Burgos%20Mirian%20Noemi%20%281%29.pdf ;

Carla Lucia Tandazo Tandazo, Univercidad Tecnica Machala — http://repositorio.utmachala.edu.ec/bitstream/48000/15465/1/E-11535_TANDAZO%20TANDAZO%20CARLA%20LUCIA.pdf ;

Mariana Alvim de Sá, Abner Eutéquio Benício da Silva, Guilherme de Freitas Oliveira, Jane Aparecida da Silveira, — Pós-Graduanda em Gerenciamento de Projetos, Navus, Florianopolis — http://navus.sc.senac.br/index.php/navus/article/download/646/pdf — «Durante as pesquisas foi extremamente difícil localizar um trabalho científico (artigos, teses ou dissertações) que tratasse de gerenciamento de tempo ou produtividade de forma que não fosse atrelado a uma área específica como indústria, agronomia, saúde e outras mais.»

[BOOK_OR_AUTHOR_OR_CONCEPT_CRITICISM] Карлссон и Аренс отмечают, что GTD может быть эффективна для бизнеса. Mizruchi, University of Michigan — https://sci-hub.se/https://www.jstor.org/stable/2781691 — «Early on (p. 19), Pfeffer notes that only after a decision is carried out can we know whether it is good or bad, which implies that a decision's consequences can be known. Yet much of the book is spent, correctly in my view, pointing out the near impossibility of deciphering the consequences of a decision.», «But how do we know which is which until it is too late? In fact, the ex post facto nature of much of Pfeffer's evidence is the most troubling aspect of the book.», «Still, there is plenty here for those interested in progressive social change», «In fact, the main problem that many will have with Pfeffer's argument is his insistence on the separation of ends and means. Devious means are often necessary to accomplish decent ends, he stresses.», «I am not entirely convinced by his selective use of evidence.»

João Climaco, Universidade de Coimbra — https://digitalis-dsp.uc.pt/bitstream/10316.2/25192/1/NotasEconomicas1_artigo12.pdf?ln=pt-pt — «Therefore it is essentially focused on a behavioural analysis of the power of persons and groups in organisations. It deals only indirectly with the structural changes of a global nature which we observe nowadays both at the political and structural levels», «Nevertheless it seems to me rather reductive in perspective. As an operational researcher I am used to debating with mathematicians who never give up constructing normative or abstractive models for the decision processes, even in the more complex cases. In my opinion, they do not understand that they are irrevocably destined to failure!», «In many cases disciplines such as cognitive psychology, sociology and political science have an important role to play. The position of Pfeffer lies in the opposite extreme of the mathematicians.»

1. Власть и влияние. Политика и управление в организациях (Вильямс, 2007).pdf

But books that criticize the status quo while suggesting that little can be done about it are poorly placed to show a way forward.»

Ks. Andrzej Makaro, doktorant Katedry Historii Filozofii Nowożytnej i Współczesnej KUL — https://ojs.tnkul.pl/index.php/rf/article/download/13538/13345 — «ie są to poglądy szczególnie oryginalne i odkrywcze. Podziela je zapewne więk-szość ludzi czynnie zajmujących się nauką, dopóki nie zaczną filozofować. Rozdział poświęcony relatywizmowi poznawczemu w filozofii nauki również nie przynosi nowa-torskich rozwiązań. Jest to zdecydowanie najsłabsza partia książki. Widać wyraźnie, że Sokal i Bricmont zdecydowanie lepsi są w szczegółowych analizach, niż w szeroko za-krojonych syntezach.», «Klucz do odpowiedzi na to pytanie leży być może w niespójnych deklaracjach autorów na temat tego, czego dowieść chcieli. Raz bowiem piszą, że celem ich jest wyłącznie wykazanie, iż postmodernistyczni intelektualiści nadużywająw swych publikacjach pojęć z zakresu nauk ścisłych, co jednak nie podważa pozostałej części ich twórczości (s. 10). Kilka stronic dalej deklarują zaś wprost: „To właśnie jest naszym celem – chcemy powiedzieć, że król jest nagi” (s. 19).»

[REVIEW_HIGH_POSITIVE][REVIEW_LONG][REVIEW_META] Jairo José da Silva, UNESP — http://pepsic.bvsalud.org/scielo.php?script=sci_arttext&pid=S1517-24302004000100005 — «Mas quem quer que leia com atenção e sem parti pris o livro de Sokal e Bricmont há de reconhecer, se não lhe falta honestidade intelectual, que os autores são extremamente cautelosos com suas críticas, sempre muito bem focadas e substanciadas, evitando generalizações indevidas e extrapolações indesejadas, e que, além disso, ambos identificam-se como homens de esquerda, que até simpatizam com certos objetivos da crítica cultural, mas que se recusam a cooptar com métodos desonestos de convencimento (que não podem ser chamados de argumentação), erros grosseiros e mistificação desenfreada.», «Segundo Jesus de Paula Assis, Sokal confundiu indevidamente esses dois relativismos, jogando na mesma vala comum Feyerabend e Derrida. Ademais, segundo o autor, Sokal escolheu um adversário fraco para o seu "experimento", já que, ainda segundo ele, Social Text é uma revista inexpressiva nas áreas de filosofia e sociologia da ciência. Há outras críticas pertinentes nesse artigo de Jesus de Paula Assis. De fato, não se pode negar, como ele acha que Sokal nega, que há estudos sérios sobre os condicionantes sociais da produção científica.»

[REVIEW_LONG] Robert F. Barsky, University of Western Ontario — https://sci-hub.se/10.2307/3685422 — «Alan Sokal's hoax has served as a protest against the collapse in standards of scholarship and intellectual responsibility with which vast sectors of the humanities and social sciences are currently afflicted. Significantly, some of the most biting commentary has come from distinguished voices on the Left, showing that when it comes to transgressions as basic as these, political alliances offer no protection.», «Much of the discussion has centered on remarks by Julia Kristeva, who suggested to Le Nouvel observateur that the Sokal business was in fact part of a growing anti-French politico-economic campaign», «Sokal and Bricmont don't render any services when they tell us to keep out because we're too stupid to understand what's going on, and they don't support the Left by telling people what to think or how to interpret the world.»

[BOOK_OR_AUTHOR_OR_CONCEPT_CRITICISM][REVIEW_LONG] Костикова Анна Анатольевна, кандидат философских наук (переводчик книги) — https://www.ruthenia.ru/logos/number/1999_04/1999_4_14.htm — «Исходя из этого подобраны и объекты критики, это прежде всего те “классики” новейшей французской философии, которые так или иначе касались вопросов точных наук. Хотя здесь сразу стоило бы оговориться, поскольку есть повод “поймать за руку” самих критиков. В разряд иррационалистов и противников науки попадают философы принципиально отличающие свое понимание науки: Бруно Лятур, занимающийся социологией науки, действительно, в своей книге “Наука в действии” определяет науку как миф, социальный конструкт и даже не рассматривает вопрос об истинности научных концепций, но Ж. Лакану и Ю. Кристевой свойственны использование научной аргументации как престижной и самоценной.», «Несмотря на все оговорки, неутешительные выводы “узкокритического” анализа использования научных терминов, А. Сокал и Ж. Брикмон распространяют на все философское произведение в целом.», «Действительно, аргументы против Ю. Кристевой выглядят наиболее несправедливо. Во-первых, в поле критики попала работа 1967 года, студенческая статья Кристевой в журнале “Тель Кель”. Во-вторых, некорректно судить по одной-двум работам обо всей концепции в целом. В-третьих, именно к ней относятся такие явно оценочные рассуждения и сравнения типа “более эрудированная в математике, чем Лакан”, “более поверхностная, чем Лакан, в своих суждениях”.», «Есть один аспект выводов А. Сокала и Ж. Брикмона, с которыми, к счастью, а, может быть, к сожалению, трудно согласиться содержательно. Речь идет о том, что по мнению авторов книги, экспортируемая из Франции философия перечисленных авторов питает движения, которые, с точки зрения А. Сокала и Ж. Брикмона, могли обойтись без философии — это движения феминизма, черного американского большинства, сексуальных меньшинств, этнических культур и так далее.», «В целом, дискуссия — еще один повод для гордости французов своей национальной философией.»

Christian Ghasarian, Institut d’ethnologie, Université de Neuchâtel, Suisse — https://journals.openedition.org/lhomme/86 — «Comme le souligne parfaitement Yves Jeanneret, Sokal « devient auteur sans avoir à exposer et argumenter ses idées, simplement en désignant le discours des autres » (p. 154). C’est, paradoxalement, en déconstruisant la renommée de ses « cibles » qu’il sort de l’anonymat et atteint la célébrité.», «La confusion s’étend d’autant plus que l’on trouve sur le banc des accusés tous les détracteurs de la modernité (les études culturelles, les postmodernes, la pensée New Age, une certaine gauche intellectuelle, etc.), empêtrés dans le relativisme, la démission politique, l’ignorance scientifique, l’obscurité stylistique, etc., ce qui fait beaucoup de monde… Confusion aussi du fait que les accusés vont eux-mêmes s’enfermer dans le piège tendu par Sokal et, pour se défendre, se renvoyer mutuellement les accusations (le style pédant, la faiblesse argumentative, etc.) dont ils sont l’objet. Du coup, la place de l’accusé est vide et on se demande sur quoi porte vraiment le débat…», «Contre cette logique de l’oubli, Yves Jeanneret a entrepris une relecture des textes initiaux pour mieux comprendre comment, à partir de la mystification des éditeurs d’une revue, on est passé à la question de savoir si les intellectuels français sont des «imposteurs». Il en arrive à la conclusion qu’il s’agit plus d’une « querelle » que d’une « affaire », et que celle-ci relève d’abord d’un phénomène de « trivialité ». La trivialité a pour caractéristique de simplifier les choses.»

[REVIEW_LONG][REVIEW_META] Jean-Philippe Bouilloud, professor at the Ecole Supérieure de Commerce de Paris ESCP-EAP — https://sci-hub.se/10.1177/0048393102250309 — «First of all, there is the “experiment” conducted by Sokal (1996b) inSocial Text: to say that he abused an American journal is not in itselfenough, for that simply displays a major dysfunction in the evalua-tion process of articles submitted to the journal (Wacquant 1997;Latour 1997; Lynch 1998; Jeanneret 1998; Jurdant 1998; Le Bras 1997)and would not disqualify the whole logic of “cultural studies,” as theincriminated journal does not depict itself as a scientific model», «Furthermore, it has been noted (Lévy-Leblond 1998; Lynch 1998;Salanskis 1998; Mermin 1998; Fixari 1998; Charraud 1998) that Sokaland Bricmont assimilate the texts that are difficult to understand6tomeaningless texts, which leads them to disregard numerous authors,7from Hegel to Lacan or Deleuze», «Yet considering science as objective (Bricmont 1997b), Sokal andBricmont do not conceive the specific particularities of the socialsciences.», «But Sokal and Bricmont weresuspected of referring to the most extreme and reductionist “socialstudies” texts, to back their theory and henceforth support a “futilesquabble”», «It is a salutary debate,yet one whose own ambiguities and approximations tend to disqual-ify (Brian 1998). In fact, it ignores the real questions. At least one cancredit it with having opened up a vast reflection on scientism and theimage of science within the social sciences. Beyond this, it is perhapsnecessary to take seriously Sokal and Bricmont’ repeated confessionthat they do not really understand the social sciences.»

[REVIEW_LONG] André Assi Barreto, Mestrando em Filosofia pela Universidade de São Paulo — https://www3.ufrb.edu.br/seer/index.php/griot/article/download/513/234/1457 — «Nós acreditamos que qualquer trabalho acadêmico que se preze, que pretenda ser levado a sério pela comunidade acadêmica, deve primar pela clareza e pelo rigor e, consequentemente, evitar todo tipo de obscuridade, de ambiguidade e de suscetibilidade aos preconceitos e subjetividades daquele que escreve.»

<a id="NotRecommended-37"></a>
### NotRecommended

<a id="Поддержка-паранауки-4"></a>
#### Поддержка паранауки

<!--- [NOTE] Глава (или раздел) «Надежды эзотеризма» не называет эзотерику паранаукой также как и научная статья этого же автора «Трансперсональная философия ХХ века о человеке (С. Гроф и К. Уилбер)» — https://cyberleninka.ru/article/n/transpersonalnaya-filosofiya-hh-veka-o-cheloveke-s-grof-i-k-uilber . Цитата: «Современные научные представления, как это ни покажется странным, все более смыкаются с древним эзотерическим знанием в описании глубинного устройства мира.»

The style of the argument is that of an accessible conversation in which everyone is invited to join in; the content of the argument however is largely negative and depicts a conversation that is almost impossible to join.», «He is desperately trying to explain to outsiders why economics is the way it is. He wants to be held accountable by the general public for what he and his colleagues are doing inside the ivory tower, and I would say rightly so.», «A conversation that is turned inward is too easy to ignore, something that politicians are very prone to do. It is truly unfortunate that Klamer does not make this argument explicit. By introducing a concept like accountability within his theory about the conversation, he could have strengthened it greatly.», «Overall, I think that while Klamer’s characterisation might be quite appropriate for the late modernistic economic conversation of the seventies and eighties, it does not do justice to the changes in that conversation since»;

Klamer is still talking about New Classical macroeconomics; theresurgence of political economy and the rise of development and (new) institutional economics are nowhere to be seen. Still,as a field guide to thecultureof economists, it remains spot on.»

[AUTHOR_PROJECT] Institute Libertad y Democracia — https://www.ild.org.pe/

[BOOK_OR_AUTHOR_OR_CONCEPT_CRITICISM][REVIEW_LONG][REVIEW_META] Paul van der Molen, former director of Kadaster International — https://www.fig.net/resources/proceedings/fig_proceedings/fig2012/papers/ts07b/TS07B_vandermolen_5503.pdf — «Especially the academia sought publicity to render scientific evidence that de Soto’s solution will not work, such as 'de Soto's solution not for South Africa' (B. Cousins), ‘The De Soto Delusion’ (Gravois) or 'The wrong prescription for the wrong malady' (Bromley) to name a few.», «1. The experiences so far.De Soto neglects that experiences from the past demonstrate that titling does not work. // 2. Customary practices (legal pluralism).De Soto neglects the role of customary tenure and management as existing legal institutions, although not under the formal ‘bell jar’. // 3. Land distribution De Soto neglects the skew access to land in many countries. // 4. CodificationDe Soto neglects that formalizing is not a simple confirmation of informal rules. It legalizes thievery, dispossession and colonial grabbing and neglects the gender issue. // 5. Role of the State and the rule of lawDe Soto relies on political will and functional governments, while current statutory legal frameworks exclude the poor and lack of enforcement hampers providing protection. // 6. The poor De Soto neglects that the ‘poor’ are not an homogenous group (there are ‘rich’ poor, and ‘’poor’ poor) so that single solutions will not work.», «Furthermore, there are two more issues, when it comes to the evidence base. The first is, that in general most reviewers reproach de Soto of not providing any evidence for his statements», «And the second is: how did it work out in the projects in Peru, in which de Soto was involved, himself. Do they provide evidence of the chain title-credit-income? The answer is ‘hardly’ or even ‘no’»

El Comercio, «El Indecopi resolvió sancionarlo con S/.10.950 por no incluir en un mandato anterior los nombres de Mario Ghibellini y Enrique Ghersi en el libro "El Otro Sendero"» — https://elcomercio.pe/economia/peru/sancionan-hernando-soto-violacion-propiedad-intelectual-noticia-1368239/

[AUTHOR_PROJECT] «The Maddison Project has been initiated in March 2010 by a group of close colleagues of Angus Maddison, with the aim to support an effective way of cooperation between scholars to continue Maddison's work on measuring economic performance for different regions, time periods and subtopics.» — https://www.rug.nl/ggdc/historicaldevelopment/maddison/?lang=en

[POSITIVE_OR_NEUTRAL_REVIEW][REVIEW_RETELLING] Vittorio Valli, University of Turin — http://ejce.liuc.it/18242979200802/182429792008050207.pdf

[REVIEW_RETELLING] Vittorio Daniele, Università ”Magna Graecia” di Catanzaro — https://sci-hub.se/10.1016/s1698-6989(09)70129-8

[REVIEW_ONE_PAGE] Geoffrey McNicoll, Australian National University — https://sci-hub.se/10.2307/25699071 — «Maddison is not reticent in reproving other economic historians. A particular charge against many Joel Mokyr, W. D. Nordhaus, and Bradford DeLong are instanced is exaggerating economic progress since 1800 and neglecting the earlier achievements of the merchant capitalist era. Depictions of centuries of Malthusian stagnation prior to 1800, with people living "like cavemen," are "fairytale scenarios" and "hallucigenic history." (Gregory Clark, a confirmed stagnationist, counters in even sharper terms in a review of this book in the December 2009 Journal of Economic History.)»

[BOOK_OR_AUTHOR_OR_CONCEPT_CRITICISM][REVIEW_SMASHER] Gregory Clark, University of California, Davis — https://sci-hub.se/https://www.jstor.org/stable/25654039 — «There is, however, a problem at the core of the book, and indeed at the core at the whole Maddison project for at least the last ten years. All the numbers Maddison estimates for the years before 1820 are fictions, as real as the relics peddled around Europe in the Middle Ages.», «Among modern economists there is a hunger by the credulous for numbers, any numbers however dubious their provenance, to lend support to the model of the moment. Maddison supplies that market. How exactly Maddison created his numbers for many countries and epochs is never precisely clear.», «There is ample evidence, however, that incomes even of the most "primitive" societies greatly exceeded the Maddison assumption. Modern anthropologists, for example, have recorded the daily food consumption of surviving hunter-gatherer and shifting cultivation groups. The median consumption per person was 2,340 kcal per day, well above Maddison's assumed subsistence.», «The population estimates are largely drawn from Colin McElvedy and Richard Jones's Atlas of World Population History. Inspection of that source reveals that it is similarly largely a work of imagination in these earlier year. This book, for example, happily quotes estimates of the population of the Indian subcontinent for the years 1820 and earlier. Yet examination of the sources reveals there are essentially no data on population for India, at present, for the years 1820 and before. All this material is suitable for use only in the most general and qualified way.», «Despite this these numbers on GDP per capita, by country, have been widely used to lend support to theoretical models. The authors using them are happily employing as "data" what is not data at all, but the expression of one man's unexamined theory of what must have happened in the last two millennia of human history.», «Thus they are not a noteworthy attraction of the book. Maddison's latest set of numbers, laid out in the tables of this book, are his claim to fame. For the reasons given above, however, any economist with enough street savvy to resist fabulous riches offered by unknown Nigerians over the internet will equally want to steer clear of these estimates.»

[REVIEW_SMASHER] Timothy Guinnane, Yale University — https://sci-hub.se/10.2307/27647156 — «For some countries, Maddison has constructed more speculative estimates that date to the start of the Common Era. His efforts now underlie much if not most research in the empirics of long-run economic growth», «One noteworthy point in this chapter comes up again below: Maddison never seriously considers the conceptual basis of the methods his heroes employed. There is a now a more-or-less close congruence between economic theory and the way we measure economic aggregates. Nowhere does Maddison broach the topic of what someone like Petty thought he was measuring.», «For example, for the German case, most of Maddison's figures rely on W. G. Hoffmann's pioneering work in German national income accounting. Hoffmann's work had important gaps and weaknesses, some of which were acknowledged by Hoffmann himself.», «How many of Maddison's underlying sources suffer similar problems? We cannot really know. With the exception of Britain and the United States, economic historians have not devoted the requisite effort to historical national income accounting.», «The "explana tion" always has a similar flavor: one authority's estimate is "too high" or "too low." Maddison rarely provides a reasoned argument or more detailed explanation of why he thinks something is too high or low.», «A final worrying trait on display here is a ten dency to react to critics with either scorn or a point-by-point rebuttal that suggests little effort to profit from disagreement. Three appendices to chapter six amount to swipes at earlier critics (one is called "Hallucigenic History"). His rejec tion of any lessons from one particular alterna tive approach is particularly troubling. His rejec tion of any lessons from one particular alterna tive approach is particularly troubling. Robert Allen and other economic historians have assem bled a large database of wages and prices that permits reasonable estimates of real wages in many European cities for much of the period for which Maddison reports GDP estimates.»

[NO_SCEDRECO] -->
1. [Мэддисон Энгас](http://www.eco.rug.nl/GGDC/maddison/CV.html) — Контуры мировой экономики в 1—2030 гг. Очерки по макроэкономической теории (Институт Гайдара, 2012).djvu

<a id="NotRecommended-39"></a>
### NotRecommended

<a id="Анти-SJW-1"></a>
#### Анти-SJW

<!--- [NOTE] В главе 24 многократно подчёркивается «научность» аргументов Ландсбурга и дискредитируются защитники окружающей среды. На самом же деле это набор аргументов из Anti-SJW глоссария — https://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Social_justice_warrior#Anti-SJW_glossary . [REVIEW_SMASHER][NO_SCIENCE_MEDIA] Russ Walker — «In the now infamous chapter in the newly released SuperFreakonomics, Steven Levitt and Stephen Dubner manage to downplay the global warming threat, compare climate change believers to religious fanatics, and accept at face value the assertion by some pointy-headed geeks that they can save the world on the cheap.», «These are fascinating ideas. But they’re just that — ideas based on some pretty big leaps of faith, i.e. that these things can be engineered, that someone will fund them, and, moreover, that the solutions will actually do enough to cool the planet.»

[REVIEW_SMASHER][NO_SCIENCE_MEDIA] Michael Mann, Ph.D. Yale University, Department of Geology & Geophysics ( https://michaelmann.net/about/cv ) — https://www.huffpost.com/entry/nate-silver-climate-change_b_1909482 — «Super Freakonomics — a book that, perhaps better than any other, serves as a cautionary tale of the dangers that lurk when academics attempt to draw sweeping conclusions in fields well outside their area of training. In Super Freakonomics as you might guess, Levitt drew questionable conclusions about climate change and related energy issues based on an extrapolation of principles of economics way, way, way, outside their domain of applicability. Even some very basic physics calculations, for example, reveal that his dismissal of solar energy as a viable alternative to fossil fuel energy in combating climate change because of possible waste heat is total nonsense. Ray Pierrehumbert, a chaired professor himself at the University of Chicago, in the Department of Geosciences, pointed this and other serious errors out to Levitt in an open letter that concluded with a campus map showing how easy it would have been for Levitt to walk over to his office to discuss his ideas and, presumably, avoid the serious pitfalls that ended up undermining much of what he ended up saying in his book about climate change and energy policy.»
